@correct_culture_primary_score = 100
@better_than_the_alternatives_score = 50
@always_primary_score = 1000

###VANILLA FASHION###

k_fashion = { # Kingdom of Fashion from Establish a New Fashion at Court decision
	color = { 140 45 165 }
	landless = yes
	destroy_on_succession = yes
	can_be_named_after_dynasty = no
	capital = c_minas_tirith # De-Jure capital has to be somewhere, will move as characters gain the title.

	no_automatic_claims = yes
	de_jure_drift_disabled = yes
}

k_sirgala = { # Even as a titular, the Shire considers Arnor its rightful liege!
	color = { 6 95 78 }
	landless = yes
	always_follows_primary_heir = yes
	definite_form = yes

	capital = c_edhelas
	ai_primary_priority = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				culture = culture:sirrandrai
			}
			add = @always_primary_score
		}
	}
}

k_sumarieth = { 
	color = { 178 124 225 }
	landless = yes
	always_follows_primary_heir = yes
	definite_form = yes

	capital = c_pred
	ai_primary_priority = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				culture = { has_cultural_pillar = heritage_moriquendi }
			}
			add = @always_primary_score
		}
	}
}

			text = lotr_cannot_be_tribal_government_trigger
